   211	/**
   212	 * @param {HTMLElement} node
   213	 * @param {string} prop
   214	 * @param {any} value
   215	 */
   216	export function set_custom_element_data(node, prop, value) {
   217	        // We need to ensure that setting custom element props, which can
   218	        // invoke lifecycle methods on other custom elements, does not also
   219	        // associate those lifecycle methods with the current active reaction
   220	        // or effect
   221	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   222	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   223	
   224	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   225	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   226	        let was_hydrating = hydrating;
   227	        if (hydrating) {
   228	                set_hydrating(false);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        set_active_reaction(null);
   232	        set_active_effect(null);
   233	
   234	        try {
   235	                if (
   236	                        // `style` should use `set_attribute` rather than the setter
   237	                        prop !== 'style' &&
   238	                        // Don't compute setters for custom elements while they aren't registered yet,
   239	                        // because during their upgrade/instantiation they might add more setters.
   240	                        // Instead, fall back to a simple "an object, then set as property" heuristic.
   241	                        (setters_cache.has(node.nodeName) ||
   242	                        // customElements may not be available in browser extension contexts
   243	                        !customElements ||
   244	                        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())
   245	                                ? get_setters(node).includes(prop)
   246	                                : value && typeof value === 'object')
   247	                ) {
   248	                        // @ts-expect-error
   249	                        node[prop] = value;
   250	                } else {
   251	                        // We did getters etc checks already, stringify before passing to set_attribute
   252	                        // to ensure it doesn't invoke the same logic again, and potentially populating
   253	                        // the setters cache too early.
   254	                        set_attribute(node, prop, value == null ? value : String(value));
   255	                }
   256	        } finally {
   257	                set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   258	                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
   259	                if (was_hydrating) {
   260	                        set_hydrating(true);
   261	                }
   262	        }
   263	}

import subprocess, textwrap, json, os, sys, pathlib, tempfile

js = r'''
const { JSDOM } = require('jsdom');
const { set_custom_element_data } = require('./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/dom/elements/attributes.js');

const dom = new JSDOM('<!doctype html><html><body></body></html>', { pretendToBeVisual: true });

global.window = dom.window;
global.document = dom.window.document;
global.customElements = dom.window.customElements;

dom.window.customElements.define('my-built', class extends dom.window.HTMLButtonElement {
  set foo(v) { this._foo = v; }
  get foo() { return this._foo; }
}, { extends: 'button' });

const el = dom.window.document.createElement('button', { is: 'my-built' });
set_custom_element_data(el, 'foo', 'bar');

'''

+import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';

+globalThis.HTMLElement = dom.window.HTMLElement;

+  set foo(v) { this._foo = v; }
+  get foo() { return this._foo; }

+import subprocess, json, os
+
+js = r'''
+import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';
+import { set_custom_element_data } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/dom/elements/attributes.js';
+
+const dom = new JSDOM('<!doctype html><html><body></body></html>', { pretendToBeVisual: true });
+
+globalThis.window = dom.window;
+globalThis.document = dom.window.document;
+globalThis.customElements = dom.window.customElements;
+// needed by svelte's internal helpers
+globalThis.Element = dom.window.Element;
+globalThis.HTMLElement = dom.window.HTMLElement;
+
+customElements.define('my-built', class extends dom.window.HTMLButtonElement {
+  set foo(v) { this._foo = v; }
+  get foo() { return this._foo; }
+}, { extends: 'button' });
+
+const el = dom.window.document.createElement('button', { is: 'my-built' });
+set_custom_element_data(el, 'foo', 'bar');
+
+console.log(JSON.stringify({ prop: el.foo, attr: el.getAttribute('foo') }));
+'''
+
+path = '/testbed/repro.mjs'
+open(path,'w').write(js)
+
+out = subprocess.check_output(['node', path], cwd='/testbed', text=True)
+print(out)
+
+# last line is json
+lines = [l for l in out.splitlines() if l.strip().startswith('{')]
+data = json.loads(lines[-1])
+if data.get('prop') != 'bar' or data.get('attr') is not None:
+    raise SystemExit(f"FAIL: builtin custom element treated as attribute: {data}")
+print('PASS')

</diff>

+                // and this wouldn't be reached in case of undefined because of the equality check below
+                if (is_option_element && key === 'value' && value == null) {
+                        // The <option> element is a special case because removing the value attribute means
+                        // the value is set to the text content of the option element, and setting the value
+                        // to null or undefined means the value is set to the string "null" or "undefined".
+                        // To align with how we handle this case in non-spread-scenarios, this logic is needed.
+                        // There's a super-edge-case bug here that is left in in favor of smaller code size:
+                        // Because of the "set missing props to null" logic above, we can't differentiate
+                        // between a missing value and an explicitly set value of null or undefined. That means
+                        // that once set, the value attribute of an <option> element can't be removed. This is
+                        // a very rare edge case, and removing the attribute altogether isn't possible either
+                        // for the <option value={undefined}> case, so we're not losing any functionality here.
+                        // @ts-ignore

+                }

+
+                var prefix = key[0] + key[1]; // this is faster than key.slice(0, 2)
+                if (prefix === '$$') continue;

+                        const event_handle_key = '$$' + key;
+                        let event_name = key.slice(2);
+                        var delegated = is_delegated(event_name);
+
+                        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
+                                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
+                                opts.capture = true;
+                        }
+
+                        if (!delegated && prev_value) {
+                                // Listening to same event but different handler -> our handle function below takes care of this
+                                // If we were to remove and add listeners in this case, it could happen that the event is "swallowed"
+                                // (the browser seems to not know yet that a new one exists now) and doesn't reach the handler
+                                // https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/11903
+                                if (value != null) continue;
+
+                                element.removeEventListener(event_name, current[event_handle_key], opts);
+                                current[event_handle_key] = null;
+                        }
+
+                        if (value != null) {
+                                if (!delegated) {
+                                        /**
+                                         * @this {any}
+                                         * @param {Event} evt
+                                         */
+                                        function handle(evt) {
+                                                current[key].call(this, evt);
+                                        }
+
+                                        current[event_handle_key] = create_event(event_name, element, handle, opts);
+                                } else {
+                                        // @ts-ignore
+                                        element[`__${event_name}`] = value;
+                                        delegate([event_name]);
+                                }
+                        } else if (delegated) {
+                                // @ts-ignore
+                                element[`__${event_name}`] = undefined;
+                        }
+                } else if (key === 'style') {
+                        // avoid using the setter
+                        set_attribute(element, key, value);
+                } else if (key === 'autofocus') {
+                        autofocus(/** @type {HTMLElement} */ (element), Boolean(value));
+                } else if (!is_custom_element && (key === '__value' || (key === 'value' && value != null))) {
+                        // @ts-ignore We're not running this for custom elements because __value is actually
+                        // how Lit stores the current value on the element, and messing with that would break things.
+                        element.value = element.__value = value;
+                } else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
+                        set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
+                } else {
+                        var name = key;
+                        if (!preserve_attribute_case) {
+                                name = normalize_attribute(name);
+                        }
+
+                        var is_default = name === 'defaultValue' || name === 'defaultChecked';
+
+                        if (value == null && !is_custom_element && !is_default) {
+                                attributes[key] = null;
+
+                                if (name === 'value' || name === 'checked') {
+                                        // removing value/checked also removes defaultValue/defaultChecked — preserve
+                                        let input = /** @type {HTMLInputElement} */ (element);
+                                        const use_default = prev === undefined;
+                                        if (name === 'value') {

+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultValue = previous;
+                                                // @ts-ignore
+                                                input.value = input.__value = use_default ? previous : null;
+                                        } else {
+                                                let previous = input.defaultChecked;
+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultChecked = previous;
+                                                input.checked = use_default ? previous : false;
+                                        }

+                                }

+                        ) {

+                                element[name] = value;
+                                // remove it from attributes's cache
+                                if (name in attributes) attributes[name] = UNINITIALIZED;
+                        } else if (typeof value !== 'function') {
+                                set_attribute(element, name, value, skip_warning);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
+                set_hydrating(true);
+        }
